<t:tests xmlns:t="urn:zimbraTestHarness">

<t:property name="test_account1.name" value="test.${TIME}.${COUNTER}@${defaultdomain.name}"/>
<t:property name="test_account1.password" value="test123"/>
<t:property name="search.name1" value="Search01${TIME}.${COUNTER}"/>
<t:property name="search.name2" value="Search01${TIME}.${COUNTER}"/>
<t:property name="searchName.number" value="12345${TIME}.${COUNTER}"/>
<t:property name="searchName.spchar" value="':;~!@"/>
<t:property name="searchName.spsymbol" value=";@!~"/>
<t:property name="searchName.blank" value=""/>
<t:property name="searchName.space" value="             "/>
<t:property name="searchName.spaces" value= "Test${TIME}     .Test${COUNTER}"/>

<t:property name="query01" value="in:inbox"/>
<t:property name="query02" value="in:contacts"/>
<t:property name="query03" value="in:sent"/>
<t:property name="query04" value="in:trash"/>
<t:property name="query.blank" value=""/>
<t:property name="query.space" value="             "/>
<t:property name="query.number" value="12345${TIME}.${COUNTER}"/>
<t:property name="query.spchar" value="':;~!@"/>
<t:property name="query.sometext" value="some text"/>
<t:property name="query.negative" value="-50"/>
<t:property name="query.decimal" value="10.10"/>

<t:property name="type1" value="message"/>
<t:property name="type2" value="conversation"/>
<t:property name="type3" value="contact"/>
<t:property name="type4" value="appointment"/>
<t:property name="type5" value="note"/>

<t:property name="sort1" value="dateDesc"/>
<t:property name="sort2" value="dateAsc"/>
<t:property name="sort3" value="nameDesc"/>
<t:property name="sort4" value="nameAsc"/>
<t:property name="sort5" value="subjDesc"/>
<t:property name="sort6" value="subjAsc"/>

<t:property name="uri" value="${admin.uri}"/> 

<t:test_case testcaseid="Ping" type="always" >
    <t:objective>basic system check</t:objective>

    <t:test id="ping" required="true">
        <t:request>
            <PingRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraAdmin"/>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
	     <t:select path="//admin:PingResponse"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

</t:test_case>


<t:test_case testcaseid="acct1_setup" type="always" >
    <t:objective>create test account</t:objective>

    <t:test id="admin_login" required="true" >
        <t:request>
            <AuthRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraAdmin">
                <name>${admin.user}</name>
                <password>${admin.password}</password>
            </AuthRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path="//admin:AuthResponse/admin:authToken" set="authToken"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

    <t:test required="true" >
        <t:request>
            <CreateAccountRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraAdmin">
                <name>${test_account1.name}</name>
                <password>${test_account1.password}</password>
            </CreateAccountRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path="//admin:CreateAccountResponse/admin:account" attr="id"  set="test_account1.id"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

</t:test_case>

<t:property name="uri" value="${mailclient.uri}"/>

<t:test_case testcaseid="acct1_login" type="always" >
    <t:objective>login as the test account</t:objective>

    <t:test required="true">
        <t:request>
            <AuthRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraAccount">
                <account by="name">${test_account1.name}</account>
                <password>${test_account1.password}</password>
            </AuthRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
	     <t:select path="//acct:AuthResponse/acct:lifetime"  match="^\d+$"/>
	     <t:select path="//acct:AuthResponse/acct:authToken" set="authToken"/>
	     <t:select path="//acct:AuthResponse/acct:sessionId" set="sessionId"/> 
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

</t:test_case>


<t:test_case testcaseid="CreateSearchFolderRequest1" type="smoke">
    <t:objective> Create Search Folder for query "in:inbox" and type "message"  </t:objective>

    <t:test>
        <t:request>
            <CreateSearchFolderRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraMail">
                <search name="${search.name1}" query="${query01}" types="${type1}" sortBy="dateDesc" l="1"/>
            </CreateSearchFolderRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse"/>
	     <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse/mail:search" attr="name" match="${search.name1}"/>
	     <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse/mail:search" attr="query" match="${query01}"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

</t:test_case>

<t:test_case testcaseid="CreateSearchFolderRequest19" type="functional" >
    <t:objective> Create Search Folder in Junk, Trash, Draft, user created folders and inside another search folder</t:objective>
 
    <t:test id="CreateSearchFolderRequest19a">
        <t:request>
               <GetFolderRequest xmlns = "urn:zimbraMail"/>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>            
            <t:select path="//mail:folder[@name='${globals.spam}']" attr="id" set="folder.spam"/> 
            <t:select path="//mail:folder[@name='${globals.sent}']" attr="id" set="folder.sent"/>
            <t:select path="//mail:folder[@name='${globals.inbox}']" attr="id" set="folder.inbox"/>        
            <t:select path="//mail:folder[@name='${globals.drafts}']" attr="id" set="folder.drafts"/>
            <t:select path="//mail:folder[@name='${globals.trash}']" attr="id" set="folder.trash"/>
            <t:select path="//mail:folder[@name='${globals.root}']" attr="id" set="folder.root"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

    <t:test depends="CreateSearchFolderRequest19a">
        <t:request>
            <CreateSearchFolderRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraMail">
                <search name="Search01${TIME}.${COUNTER}" query="${query01}" types="${type2}" sortBy="dateDesc" l="${folder.spam}"/>
            </CreateSearchFolderRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse"/>
            <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse/mail:search" attr="l" match="${folder.spam}"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

    <!--Create Search Folder in Trash folder-->
    <t:test depends="CreateSearchFolderRequest19a">
        <t:request>
            <CreateSearchFolderRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraMail">
                <search name="Search01${TIME}.${COUNTER}" query="${query01}" types="${type2}" sortBy="dateDesc" l="${folder.trash}"/>
            </CreateSearchFolderRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse"/>
            <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse/mail:search" attr="l" match="${folder.trash}"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

     <!--Create Search Folder in Drafts folder-->
     <t:test depends="CreateSearchFolderRequest19a">
        <t:request>
            <CreateSearchFolderRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraMail">
                <search name="Search01${TIME}.${COUNTER}" query="${query01}" types="${type2}" sortBy="dateDesc" l="${folder.drafts}"/>
            </CreateSearchFolderRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse"/>
            <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse/mail:search" attr="l" match="${folder.drafts}"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

    <!--Create Search Folder in User created folder-->
    <t:test id="CreateSearchFolderRequest19b" depends="CreateSearchFolderRequest19a">
        <t:request>
            <CreateFolderRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraMail">
                <folder name="folder${TIME}${COUNTER}" l="${folder.root}"/>
            </CreateFolderRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
           <t:select path="//mail:CreateFolderResponse/mail:folder" attr="id" set="folder.id1"/>
           <t:select path="//mail:CreateFolderResponse/mail:folder" attr="name" set="folder.name1"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

    <t:test depends="CreateSearchFolderRequest19b">
        <t:request>
            <CreateSearchFolderRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraMail">
                <search name="Search01${TIME}.${COUNTER}" query="${query01}" types="${type2}" sortBy="dateDesc" l="${folder.id1}"/>
            </CreateSearchFolderRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse"/>
            <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse/mail:search" attr="l" match="${folder.id1}"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

    <!--Create Search Folder in another search folder-->
    <t:test id="CreateSearchFolderRequest19c">
        <t:request>
            <CreateSearchFolderRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraMail">
                <search name="Search01${TIME}.${COUNTER}" query="${query01}" types="${type2}" sortBy="dateDesc" l="1"/>
            </CreateSearchFolderRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse"/>
            <t:select path="//mail:CreateSearchFolderResponse/mail:search" attr="id" set="search.id1"/>

<t:test_case testcaseid="CreateSearchFolderRequest27" type="functional" >
    <t:objective> Create Search folder with name same as another normal folder in same branch </t:objective>
    <t:steps>
        1. Create a normal folder inside inbox folder
        2. Create a search folder with same name in inbox folder
    </t:steps>  

    <t:test id="CreateSearchFolderRequest27a" depends="CreateSearchFolderRequest19a">
        <t:request>
            <CreateFolderRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraMail">
                <folder name="folder${TIME}${COUNTER}" l="${folder.inbox}"/>
            </CreateFolderRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
           <t:select path="//mail:CreateFolderResponse/mail:folder" attr="id" set="folder.id1"/>
           <t:select path="//mail:CreateFolderResponse/mail:folder" attr="name" set="folder.name1"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

    <t:test depends="CreateSearchFolderRequest27a">
        <t:request>
            <CreateSearchFolderRequest xmlns="urn:zimbraMail">
                <search name="${folder.name1}" query="${query01}" types="${type2}" sortBy="dateDesc" l="${folder.inbox}"/>
            </CreateSearchFolderRequest>
        </t:request>
        <t:response>
            <t:select path= "//zimbra:Code" match="^mail.ALREADY_EXISTS"/>
        </t:response>
    </t:test>

</t:test_case>

    <t:objective> Create Search folder inside another normal folder with name same as its parent's </t:objective>
    <t:steps>

        2. Create a search folder with same name inside the created folder
